Mr. Sun Myung Moon's Words Compilation Committee

Foreword
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
The Messiah and Us
Most ordinary people living in this world do not realize that they need a Messiah. Only those who engage in religious life come to know this. Humans must seek the path of salvation. In this world, we humans are incomplete. We seek the value of a completed human being or the standard of an ideal character, but those who seek are within the realm of fallenness.

Humans Who Have Lost God
There may be many who think that their efforts in this world will lead to fulfillment, but we know well that fallen humanity, no matter how much it demands, cannot reach the standard of completion. The desire to achieve completion is ultimately a result of the fall. The fall is the problem. Humans have not stood as beings with original ideal values; they have lost that standard of value and have fallen away. Therefore, humanity living on this earth must seek that value again from the place they have fallen to. No matter how much effort is made, unless one stands on that standard, one cannot attain the highest value that one seeks, which is the ideal or the completion of character as the greatest human being. This is the desire of humanity itself.

What humans desire is, of course, but if God exists, He must also desire it. Therefore, if God does not elevate ignorant humans to the highest standard of value, His original purpose of creation will not be fulfilled. Thus, God desires from behind, and fallen humans aim for the future and seek it. Unless the time that aligns with that standard comes, it cannot fulfill God's ideals, nor can it satisfy the highest values that humans desire as human beings.

However, humanity living in this world does not certainly know whether God truly exists or not. This is the problem. If one knew that God exists, there would be no need for explanation or anything else. There would be no need to teach. There would be no need to study any direction or concept of purpose. 

Each individual, with the single-minded desire to belong to God, would naturally reach the purpose that God desires. Therefore, if one knows for certain that God exists, everything is resolved. Issues regarding individuals, families, tribes, nations, or the world become problems, but even the problems of the entire world can be resolved. If one knew for sure that God exists, there would be no need for humanity to seek anything new centered on humans on this earth. Therefore, if we love one another towards God, and live together as companions, we will naturally reach the world of purpose, both individual and overall. Thus, the problem lies in the fact that we have lost God. By losing God, we have inevitably lost the perfect or highest values given by God. This is the fall.

We have neither seen nor heard of Adam and Eve or our ancestors falling. However, we were born into the world of the consequences of the fall. Therefore, the present age in which we live, this world, is under the realm of fallenness. This is the problem. We must break free from this realm of fallenness. We must overcome it. The question is how to overcome it as individuals. Once individuals have overcome, they must also overcome centered on families. But it does not stop at families. We must go until we overcome the highest standards of tribes, nations, the world, and the universe. Here, the realm of fallenness occupies everything. The question of how to correct this is a significant issue that we fallen humans must solve.

It is not possible to accomplish this by investing everything in the present age. It cannot be done by the power of a nation or the power of the world. As long as it is surrounded and bound within the realm of fallenness, it is impossible to achieve liberation or escape from it centered on itself.

The Necessity of the Messiah
Therefore, humanity must now rely on a third party. This is where the necessity of religion arises. 

If an absolute loving God exists, He wants to correct all these circumstances. This has also been the demand of humanity through history. Along with this demand, if God exists, He does not want to place humanity in such a position. That is not God's original ideal. This has become an unavoidable result, and unless God Himself raises it to the original standard, He cannot establish His authority as the absolute God.

For each of us humans, regardless of the harshness of our circumstances, we strive to achieve what we have planned. This is the desire of fallen humans. From the perspective of the original absolute God, leaving His ideals unestablished and unfulfilled is a matter of prestige and authority. Therefore, God cannot leave fallen humans as they are. Hence, the issue of God's providence arises because He must save fallen humans.

Humans want to be saved. God wants to save them. The two must align. The question is how to fulfill the standard where both parties meet at one point. That one point is not the same as being dragged into individual environments. It is not a point centered on family either. It must be a point centered on the nation and the world, where everyone must be drawn into that unified point. God cannot help but seek such a point.

Humans also desire that point, but when will that standard be realized on earth? This is the problem. When that point is established, of course, individual perfection will be achieved. Family standards will also be established. The issues of nations and the world can also be liberated from this standard. This is the position we must reach.

Who will take responsibility for this standard? Can humans take responsibility and accomplish it? Absolutely not. Can God Himself take responsibility and carry it out? If that were possible, this issue would have been resolved without passing through the historical process of six thousand or several thousand years. This is not a matter that God directly intervenes in and resolves. The problem here is that if fallen humans cannot accomplish it, then God cannot fulfill it either. So, who will accomplish this is the question.

This is where the existence of the Messiah becomes necessary. Now, when we look at the world situation, even setting aside the religious realm, will the ideal society that humanity desires be realized in general society or in various countries? This is the problem.

Will the ideal world or paradise that has been sought through religion be realized in our human world? We have entered a stage where we must ask this question again. However, even if we try to go beyond that questioning position, we cannot surpass it. We must break through the depths of that dilemma in our lives.

If God exists, we want to receive new guiding principles in the religious realm. If God exists, humanity hopes for a new leader of the times. That is the earnest desire of all humanity.

Throughout the historical process, humans have tried in various ways to realize the thoughts of saints and righteous people. However, there has been no success or fulfillment of the standard of hope as a result of those efforts. We have reached a conclusion similar to despair through that. In this regard, it has become evident that no human power or thought can achieve the world that humanity demands.

Therefore, we must find that one person who makes both God and humanity happy and follow him. God will also be pleased with the way He raises that person and must help him. If he is a central being, this will be God's joy. It will undoubtedly be the joy of humanity as well. This is the position of the Messiah.

Be Thoroughly Aware of the Concept of Fallenness
It is because of the fall that the Messiah has become necessary. If there had been no fall, there would be no need for a Messiah. Because of the fall, we have lost God. Because of the fall, we have lost the original values of humanity. If there had been no fall, the original values of humanity would have been possessed from the moment of birth. In this case, there would be no need for God's action again. There would be no need for it. It is already a position that is filled. There is nothing more to be filled. If centered on God, if humans had become one centered on God, there would be nothing unknown. For us, education regarding this fundamental issue is unnecessary.

What is the fundamental issue regarding humanity? It is about eating. Then it is about living. And after living, it ultimately leads to the issue of love.

Have you learned to eat since you were born? From the moment you are born from your mother's womb, you naturally eat as a natural phenomenon. Or you must absorb it. There is no need for education there. You come to know that when you approach the object, you will naturally eat.

Thus, we seek ideals such as eating, living, and loving naturally. We do not need education regarding these natural phenomena. Even insects know how to reproduce naturally. To give another example, when a daughter gets married, parents do not fundamentally need to teach her about love. She will come to know it naturally. According to the demands of nature, passing through the process of purpose, encountering the world of three-dimensional senses and values is the original being that is not fallen.

It is because of the fall that this has been reversed. Because it has been reversed, we must set it right again. When humans are born, their heads are down, and their bottoms are up, but we must turn this back around. They have the shape of humans but are not human. Therefore, they stand in such a position. It is because of the fall that they are caught in such a fate.

Thus, we must be thorough in our understanding of the concept of fallenness. What must we feel first to return to the original state? The question is how to firmly experience the concept of fallenness rather than desiring the Messiah. A person locked in prison cannot wish for liberation or release if they do not know they are in prison.

First of all, we humans are seeking something. We are hoping for liberation. If we are certain of that, then why has it come to this? It is the result of the fall. It is because of the fall. Therefore, we must be thorough in the concept of fallenness. The more thorough we are in the concept of fallenness, the stronger our desire becomes.

If we knew that a savior, that is, a redeemer, was coming, we would already be preparing one hundred percent before he arrives. There would be no need for explanation. We would certainly have the desire to prepare in every way possible to meet him. Therefore, what is the mission of religion? It is to teach how to strongly experience the concept of fallenness, the concept of fallen humans, and sinners in any way possible. This is the mission of religion.

Among the young people who claim to be members of the Unification Church, there are many who do not know they are fallen beings. Especially for those who have just entered the Unification Church, it is even more so. They do not even think about what the fall is. Even if their ancestors fell, they think of it as a story from millions of years ago. They wonder what relation that fall has to them. It does not resonate in their hearts. Therefore, the problem is how humans feel strongly about the concept of fallenness, such as how they fell.

If one knows for sure that they have fallen, they will seek the savior without needing to be taught. Even if told to close their eyes, they will open them. Even if told to turn their face that way, they will already be facing it. This is how it happens.

However, throughout the historical process, humanity has not been thorough in such concepts. Even while engaging in religious life, various actions have been taken. After achieving individual liberation, one must achieve family liberation, and after achieving family liberation, one must achieve liberation of the tribe, nation, world, and the universe, ultimately liberating God as well. What, is there such a strange statement as liberating God? It is possible.

If children are imprisoned, the children may be physically imprisoned, but the parents are emotionally imprisoned. Is that not so? The child knows nothing and may eat an extra lunch box because they are hungry, sleeping soundly at night. But the parents are not like that. Until liberation, they are emotionally bound more than the child.

Men exist for women, and women exist for men.
When we think about this, it is certain that God has a relationship with humanity. That God, who has a relationship, truly exists, but ordinary humans do not know about Him. What kind of relationship could there be between God and humans? God is the loving parent. If God is the center of love, what kind of love relationship will He establish with us humans? This is a serious question.

There are quite a few women here, so I will ask the women. If a woman was born with the thought, "What if there are no men...," would she have been born? Would she be born? "No, she would not be born." If there are hundreds of millions, tens of billions, or hundreds of billions of women, that would all be sorted out completely within a century. If that happens, it would be a big problem. In light of that, women, do not be complacent. The basis for self-pride is possible because men are present; what would happen if there were no men? One person's...
If there were only men, the war among women would continue for decades. Think about that. If so, it would be a big problem. 

When a woman is born, did she ever think about whether there would be a man or not? Was she born for the sake of women? Think about this. Women are not born for women. The beautiful appearance of a woman is not for the sake of other women. For whom is it? You must come to a conclusion. 

It is for men. Without men, women have no value. Not even a penny's worth. The restoration of women's values cannot be achieved by women themselves. The value of women is determined by the existence of men. Therefore, without an absolute standard, there can be no value. 

Now, let’s say there is a man with an excellent physique. Even if a man boasts, "I am the first handsome man like this in Japan," the physique he possesses was developed for someone else. It is not his own. Men must remember this. The appearance that men boast about is not for themselves. However, among the youth, there are none who think this way. If we analyze from the very moment of birth, men were born for women. It is unfortunate, but it cannot be helped. Even if they dislike it, they cannot avoid it. If not, try living alone. Those people would be separated from the world and gathered on an island, and within a century, they would completely disappear. In the end, men are not born for men. This must be understood.

No matter how excellent a man may be, no matter how strong and resolute he is to trample the world under his feet, he was born for women. Therefore, the value of women is immense. 

The teacher standing here is the same. The teacher speaks extensively. There are various problems. In Korea, in Japan... This time, I met about ten senators in the United States and declared war. Such things happen in the United States. Nearly 200 million Americans are not fulfilling their mission, so I am trying to save America by myself. I am trying to start such a thing. This has become a problem. The United States is looking at Mr. Moon with colored glasses, wondering what kind of man he is. No matter how grand the activities are, if there is no counterpart, it is pitiful. In this light, the value of mothers rises.

When we think this way, where do we belong? What kind of person am I? This is a serious matter. Where is the path one must take? The path of men is not to go among men. Even if they dislike it, they must zigzag along with women. Women are destined to walk with men. Men must walk the path with women. Women must walk with men. Therefore, one must not demand a reality centered on oneself. We must connect and save each other. This is a value that must be held as a fundamental expectation of existence since we were born as humans. It is not just humans. In all phenomena, there is relativity. However, that relativity does not exist to form a standard of existence centered on oneself. Value appears where there is mutual entanglement and agreement with others. This cannot be denied.

If Japan is to be considered valuable... If Japan has a stronger sense of purpose in which the sovereign and the people become one, Japan will not perish. However, if the national sovereignty goes in one direction while the people go in another, the more it moves, the more it tilts. The more it acts, the weaker it becomes. This is a principle.

Therefore, when we think this way, the essence of humanity, the 3.4 billion people, can be unified and concluded as men and women, that is, two people. Broadly speaking, it can be divided into two: women and men. 

Even though Westerners are here, and they have blue eyes and blonde hair, that does not matter. People are the same. When there is sadness, they shed tears. When there is joy, even if told not to, they open their mouths. No matter how unsightly their teeth may be, they cannot help but smile. That is how it is.

When we divide in this way, we distinguish between men and women. Men and women must first make each other happy. If those two stand together, shouting in the same direction, then it is not a path of unhappiness. Human happiness does not come flying down from the heavens like a goblin's dance. It does not exist as long as we cannot satisfy each other among comrades.

In this view, no matter how many humans there are, it is limited to men and women. The past was like that. The present is like that. The future must also be like that. It will absolutely be so. The crucial question is how to distribute this absolute standard of male and female value. Here, how can the two hold hands together and overcome their realities through good value standards and fulfill their joy? 

If the standards are not fulfilled, the nation cannot exist, regardless of what happens to it. An ideal world cannot come into being without fulfilling those standards.

The problem is oneself. 

When we think this way, the problem becomes simple. In the end, the world is not the problem. It is not the clan or the family; it is oneself that is the problem. It is oneself that is the issue. 

If one has a heart that loves and is loved by the world forever, one becomes a child of God. If women stand in a position where they forever hate or dislike, not finishing their grudges, then they are not on God's side. In this light, this world is a world of evil. 

To conclude, ultimately, it is our individual selves that are the problem. The individual is the issue. Then, what about oneself? History has a past, a present, and a future. In this context, where does one stand? 

The present is the embodiment of the past. The past serves as the starting point of the present. It is the center of the current age. This must be clearly understood. The present is the starting point for the future. If one stands in a negative position compared to the future, the so-called value cannot be fulfilled. Today is the center. No matter how difficult the world may be, does one have the power to move, or not? The action that one must perform as a motive has the power to apply, but it is not in a position to act. That central value system of oneself is the problem. 

Even if there is a future, it starts from oneself. Then, what kind of man would God favor? Would He favor someone who only pursues ideals? Is there a present without a past? Is there a result without a cause? That ignores the principles. Seeking a value system with only ideals, if there were a perfect or complete person, that would only be worth one-third of a point. If that person were given a hundred points, the one who gave it would be worthless. 

You must understand that. Reality is the problem. In reality, if one can say, "History! Follow me. Present! Follow me. Future! Start from me as the standard," then that person has the value to command history to follow them. That person is indeed a historical victor. If, in tracing history, all significant events are resolved by that person, and they have become the center of the current age, then they are in a position that surpasses everything in this world. That is the issue. 

The Satan that binds humanity. 

If God exists, there must be a relationship with humanity and the past, present, and future. However, the question is why such a God could not become one. In the past, God wanted to communicate with humanity. But because of the fall, because humanity became evil, that could not happen. In the present age, God wants to live with all people based on His central standard. But why can’t it happen? Originally, God wanted that, but why did it not come to pass? 

It became this way because of the fall. That fall was not something humanity wanted. So, who is the one who caused the fall? Is it God or humanity? 

Humanity did not want to fall. From the moment you young people were born, you did not stand in a position saying, "I will become a bad child. I will become a delinquent. I will become a gangster." No one is born wanting that. It happened due to some motivation. 

However, the true heart of humanity does not desire evil. If there is someone to teach and manage, even if one wants to be bad, they cannot become so. Wanting to be bad is because there is a motivation for that evil. What your parents say is, "You must associate with good friends. You must meet good teachers." They teach such things. 

In that way, if there were a concept of liking evil in humanity before the fall, then God's principle of creation would be flawed. From the result of evil, evil was not achieved by humanity's motivation. It was not something God sought and achieved. It was brought about by some cause. What is that cause? In our religious circles, it is referred to as demons or Satan. There is such a thing as Satan. 

When asking someone who has done various bad things, "Why do you do such bad things?" they often reply, "I did not want to, but I unconsciously felt that way and acted." Many people respond this way. 

You may not know this because you have not experienced the suffering of being in prison, but the teacher is an expert in that area. No one who is in prison admits that they did bad things because they are bad. When asked why they did such things, they first say society is bad. If society is bad, then why did you become so bad? Many say they did it unconsciously. This indicates that there is someone who caused that result. 

That is Satan, the originator of evil. So, they deeply regret and feel indignant. They must correct this. Even if it means sacrificing oneself, they are in a fate where they must resolve this somehow. If there were no one who caused the fall, it would truly be good, but if there is someone who caused the fall, it is a big problem. This means that there is always a powerful overseer watching over those trying to escape. 

When we look at it this way, if one wants to break down the place where they are imprisoned, they must fight. The opponent they are fighting against is incredibly skilled; it cannot be expressed in words. They are very adept. For thousands of years, they have slandered even God and humanity, wielding evil as they please. 

To illustrate such a case, one could say that Satan and a person are like the most famous sumo wrestler in Japan and a kindergarten child. No matter how much one breaks down the place they are trapped in and escapes, as long as that sumo wrestler is there, they will soon be trapped again. That would be the end. If he were not there, it might seem there would be a way to solve the problem, but if there is a supervisor, it is impossible to solve the problem, no matter how much people form alliances. Is that not so? Therefore, there are troublesome beings for both God and humanity. If God exists, liberation is not the issue. Liberation can happen in an instant. It thoroughly collides with God, having an organizational network that spans the past, present, and future. When slandered against God, if that slander cannot be denied, one must negotiate with it. If such content is brought up in slander, God cannot do anything about it. 

The non-principled world governed by Satan. 

When we think centered on God, the issue is Satan. What has Satan been a problem centered around until now? God created all things based on this principle, so it is the principle that governs. There is that principle. If Satan has seized that principle, they can slander at any time. In cases that do not align with that principle, slander can occur at any moment. Thus, the issues referred to in the Unification Church arise from the non-principled perspective. 

That is the world of the fall. Did God wish for that? He did not wish for it. However, a non-principled central figure appeared and has been slandering based on the principle's trajectory. If such a problem arose in the world, what would God do? Until the non-principled is denied, the authority of the principle does not arise. Until it is denied... Who will deny it? It is not God who will do it. 

God cannot do it. Therefore, humans who are being dragged along in a non-principled manner must meet the conditions to deny it. Thus, the non-principled things are not those who should follow God. They are not those who stand in the realm of God's intervention. However, since they take on the form of the principle, they stand by the standards of God's principle, but God cannot intervene in this. If such a problem arises, God cannot do anything about it either. If humans stand on the relative standard of the non-principled, they must solve this problem themselves. If one gets caught in such a standard, even God cannot do anything about it. This is the resentment of history. 

What was the center around which this happened? You have learned about the theory of the fall, but the principle of the fall does not originally exist. So why does the principle of the fall exist? It is based on the non-principle. If humanity did not fall and continued along that path, it would not exist. 

If the fall occurred in matters other than love, the principle of the fall would not be established. It would be restored immediately. If a hand were cut off, it could be done without it. A leg could be absent. The fundamental issue is caught up. That is the issue of love. 

If that precious person, who should truly be a princess, is taken by the monster of a bandit in that country and forms a love relationship, what should be done in such a case? The king must behead those two evil ones. But what if beheading them means that no children will ever be born again? That would be the result. 

Normally, one should never take such a method, but if it has come to that, what should be done? If the princess has not designated anyone as a partner, there is even less room for forgiveness. Even if there is a fiancé, there is no way to forgive. If one cuts them off, that would be the end. Then the lineage would disappear. The lineage of humanity would vanish. What disappears is not the principle. Humanity must eternally exist, so cutting them off cannot be done. How tragic is that king who stands in such a position? If it has come to that, it would be simple to kill them. If such a problem exists for the Japanese people, it can be dealt with by national law. Even if they are not there, there are plenty of people. But if that person is the only one, what will be done? It is a big problem. 

If humanity has fallen for reasons other than that, then God does not need 6,000 years, nor even 6 days. Because of such a problem... The man who committed the sin is undoubtedly a sinner. The woman is undoubtedly a sinner. Because they committed that sin, it is principled that they must be punished. That is the principle of the universe. If there is someone who resists that punishment, the king will reconsider. One must never become such a counterpart. It is only natural to be punished; one must be grateful even if beaten. There can be no other way to be forgiven than that. If one stands in a position of complaint and resistance, the path to forgiveness is blocked. 

Satan is the god of the non-principle.
In the Bible, there is a passage where Satan consults with God. God is the God of principles, while Satan is the god of non-principles. It has indeed become strange. Can a non-principle god interfere with the God of principles? It cannot. Can a non-principle god interfere with the dominion of the good God? It cannot. Therefore, when fallen humans submit to the non-principle evil god, Satan, without a doubt, God will say, "Make arrangements. Bring them out." And when trying to go to the side of the God of principles, the evil god, Satan, will say, "Take them back." Because of these occurrences, even if one dislikes it, they must meet daily.

One must make a distinction. We are currently in a position of division. So, in making this division, which side is internal and which side is external? That becomes the issue. From the perspective centered on God, Satan is external, and God is internal. Thus, humans themselves are drawn to their respective sides.

The Battle of Conscience and Flesh
We humans also possess two aspects: conscience and flesh. In the world, it is known that there is not a single person without a conscience. Is there anyone who claims to be without a conscience? "No." Everyone has their own conscience. Have you seen a conscience? No one has seen it. However, we know it exists. No one has seen the flesh either. This is the problem. While we absolutely know that we have a conscience, no one has seen it. We absolutely see the flesh and know it exists. This is the problem.

Thus, when viewed proportionally, which is stronger: the absolute knowledge of something that has never been seen or the absolute knowledge of something that has been seen? The side of the flesh is ahead. This is the issue.

You are the same. When you feel hungry, does your conscience recognize it because you are hungry, or does your flesh recognize it because it is hungry? The flesh, everyone prioritizes the flesh. What we desire is to see, meet, and live. What can we call this center? The part that touches is not internal but external. However, the resolution of what is felt and the source of its fruition is not the flesh but the conscience.

This has now become a philosophical issue. Therefore, where is the boundary between the place where God meets humans and the place where Satan meets humans? The boundary is oneself. Do not be afraid of global wars. The two major camps are fighting daily centered around oneself, and there is nothing that can be done about it. Morning and night, dozens or even hundreds of times a day. Even a single wrong word can become an issue. At that moment, what can be blamed or reproached? Is it the flesh or the conscience? The reproaching entity is the conscience.

Thus, it is a battle. Has the conscience ever weakened to the point where the flesh says, "Oh, conscience! What are you doing?" It is the opposite. The conscience attacks the flesh, saying, "You shouldn't do that." Then, in this world, are there proportionally more conscientious people or more unconscientious people? When we think about it, there are proportionally more conscientious people. They commit all sorts of wrongdoings while feeling the pangs of conscience. They are engaged in that battle.

So, where do we seek the standards of education such as religion or culture? It is the power of the conscience. That is the function of education or religion. And what does it do? It occupies the foothold of the flesh. That is the goal. The boundary between the good and the evil arises. This must be clearly established.

The Center of Good and Evil is Oneself
What is oneself? Evil. Then what is evil? It is the realm that should be governed by God based on good and the realm that should be governed by Satan. What boundary will divide these? This must be clearly established. That is oneself. One must think about this.

Even when eating breakfast, depending on where one goes after eating, the food can become food of evil or food of good. At night, resting can become a rest of evil or a rest of good, depending on what one does during that rest. A moment connects the two.

The center of good and evil is not the world. The center of good and evil is not God. Satan is the center of evil. More than that, it is humanity that encompasses both. When viewed this way, humans are more excellent than God and more excellent than Satan. The center of good and evil is oneself. This must be made clear.

Therefore, what is more frightening than God is humanity. What is more frightening than Satan is humanity. Depending on human actions, a nation can be destroyed. Even if one-third of the citizens are good, they can be wiped out in an instant. One must understand this. Who is the frightening one? It is oneself. What happens when these frightening beings unite? The issue of unity does not arise. The starting point of the battle begins here. One must think about this. Since it started from here, the union of external people naturally occurs. The union of internal people also naturally occurs. Therefore, in this world, there must arise two major currents of thought. One denies good, and the other denies evil; such thoughts must inevitably arise on earth. That time is the last days, and those last days are the present age.

Can God exist centered on materialistic history? To deny that value from one end is an act of the enemy's authority. The more malicious one is, the stronger that power becomes. The side of good does not work that way. This has become the confrontation between communism and democracy. Such results must arise.

Occupy the Flesh and Satan
Where did this begin? It connects from oneself. When viewed centered on oneself, this is oneself being at the forefront. Therefore, the desire of humanity is to stand at the global forefront. Thus, one must have the conviction that they are the foremost leaders in overcoming sins historically, presently, and in the future. If one is to live, they must resolve all past issues, all present issues, and all future issues. How do we discern and resolve this? There lies the issue of the future. There are two major problems: occupying the flesh in reality and occupying the unseen Satan. Do you understand? One must fight against this. What is the foremost battle? It is the flesh. The path of restoration
Through the fall, we inherited the blood of Satan. If the human ancestors Adam and Eve had not fallen, they would have become sinless children of God, but due to the fall, they became children of Satan. Originally, humans were meant to be governed only by God. God alone should have been the master of humanity. However, by forming an illicit relationship with Satan, Satan became the master of humanity.

The principle teaches that love involves control and dominion. Therefore, even if it is illicit love, Satan has the right to claim ownership over humanity. However, according to the principle of creation, God is ultimately the original master of humanity, so both God and Satan can claim ownership over humanity. However, it is physically impossible to divide Adam into two and have God and Satan share him. Therefore, God established a rule from a principled perspective to separate humanity into two. That is, through the internal existence of God and the external existence of creation, God set the rule of separation based on the relationship of internal and external and the subject-object relationship. Thus, God separated the fallen Adam and Eve through the two children they bore.

Cain represents Satan, and Abel represents the position of the sinless Adam. God placed the second son (Abel) in the internal position. Abel is the representation of the second love, meaning he is the embodiment of the love established between Adam and Eve.

Abel is the fruit of the second love. Cain is the fruit of the first love and represents Satan. Therefore, God took the second son, Abel, because the relationship between Eve and Adam is closer than that between Eve and the archangel.

However, the original order of command was to start from God to Adam, and then from Adam to the archangel, so in this case, it must go from God to Abel, and then from Abel to Cain. This is the position and relationship of restoration. There, God first restores this formula to regain the lost principle.

Due to the act of the fall, humanity's bloodline was crossed. In other words, the blood of Satan has occupied humanity's bloodline. Therefore, this restoration must go back to the source, and for that reason, the second son Abel must restore the birthright of the first son.

The fall originated from the womb of the mother. Therefore, restoration must also occur in the womb of the mother. Since that was the source and starting point of evil, in restoration, one must return to that cause. Thus, God sought to carry out the providence of restoring the birthright of the first son through these two brothers. That is, Cain must go down to the position of Abel, and Abel must rise to the position of Cain, that is, the position of the first son. However, Cain killed Abel. This act is a repetition of the act of the fall during the time of Adam and Eve. Instead of being in the position of restoration, he ended up standing in the position where the angel governed Adam. This part is difficult to understand, so I would like to explain it with a diagram.

With brothers of different ages, the distance is too great, so God sought a closer person. That is, He intended to carry out this restoration providence from a closer standard, a more original standard. The best method would be to return the lives of Cain and Abel back to the womb of the mother, but that is physically impossible.

This is structured like overlapping centers. I and II correspond to each other. The part of I is repeated in the realm of II. Therefore, God's providence appeared through the twin brothers Esau and Jacob. It is the same principle applied to Cain and Abel, where Jacob must return to the position of the elder brother, and Esau must go down to the position of the younger brother. The mother of the twin brothers was Rebekah. When she was pregnant, the two babies in her womb struggled with each other.

So she went to God and asked Him. God said, "Two nations are in your womb, and two peoples will be separated from your body. One people will be stronger than the other, and the elder will serve the younger." This was God's own proclamation.

Jacob's mission
Jacob was establishing the condition to avoid accusation. He could buy the birthright from Esau with bread and lentil stew. Therefore, even though Jacob took the birthright from Esau, Satan could not accuse him. Thus, the birthright was restored, and the blessing from the father was given to Jacob. However, Esau was so angry that he wanted to kill Jacob, just as Cain had done before.

Jacob was in a position where he had to restore the position of Abel that had been lost, as well as the position of Adam. That is why he had to flee to Haran for 21 years. Because of that, he could not completely fulfill all his missions during that time. After 21 years, he gathered his wealth and returned to his homeland, the land of Canaan. Looking at the process of the fall, the mother led the act of the fall, and the son completed it, so together they caused humanity to fall. Therefore, in the process of restoration, one must walk the opposite path. Thus, during Jacob's time, the mother Rebekah and the second son Jacob cooperated to achieve their goal.

Jacob's mission was to restore the position of Adam that had been invaded by the angel, and also to restore the position of Abel that had been killed by Cain. And Jacob had to return to the position of Esau and subdue Esau, who had gone down to the position of Jacob.

So what was Jacob's mission after 21 years? You must think about how Adam disappeared. Because restoring Adam's position is primarily the most important mission for him. That is why the angel could bless Jacob.

What is Jacob's second mission? It is to win against the angel. Thus, through victory, that is, internal victory, the position of Adam was restored. Then, under that condition, he was in a position to restore the position of Abel. In this way, Esau went down to the position of the younger brother, and Jacob rose to the position of the elder brother. However, when I trace the heart of the Father, who turned back with tears and suppressed His aching heart to look again at Jesus, who was destined to die on the cross and could not help but bless Him, I ask you, Father, to remember once again the pitiful Korean people. O heaven, do not depart from this land. Do not forsake this nation. Even if you may forsake this nation and countless denominations, I feel that the Unification Church, which wishes to become a sacrifice for this nation and countless denominations, must not be forsaken.

Father, we may appear to you as a similar group before your heart, which is deeply wounded by distrust, but we hope that you will watch over us for 10 or 20 years, and at this time, we resolve that, Father, please believe in us once again. We repent of our past as children of distrust and ask you to believe in us as children of faith. Although our faces may be rough and our bodies may be clad in tattered rags, we have not lost our hearts and integrity. Please see this, Father, and remember us.

When we come to this historical misery, shedding tears along with heaven and arriving at this land, please allow us to stand in a position where we cannot be a leader of comfort or a leader of counsel. Now, we must not walk the path of destruction, and we must not walk the path that heaven forsakes; therefore, we must warn that we cannot become children of distrust before you, holding on to these people morning and evening, and we must teach that we cannot become traitors and betrayers on the path of struggle.

Father, at this time, we bow before you. We have understood what you require. I must not become one who cannot believe in myself. I must firmly believe in myself. I must clearly know that I cannot change, even if heaven and earth change.

Father, on the foundation of the history of distrust, if you have a group that can believe day and night and for a lifetime, a hundred years, or even a thousand years, then I believe that through that group, heaven will weave a new history. This son standing here has already sworn to stand in such a place. The sons and daughters gathered here also swear at this time to become such sons and daughters, so Father, please remove all traces of violation caused by distrust from their hearts and allow them to return to the foundation of faith, holding the seeds of faith in their hearts, and become your sons and daughters who run towards the world of faith.

Father, I once again ask you to bring the children of unification scattered around the world before you. Please, please do not let them become people who die for their own interests. Let them become people who die for your interests. They must not become a group that dies within the boundaries of any individual, family, or nation. We understand that unless a group goes the path of death for the world and humanity, for heaven, the kingdom of justice cannot see the light on this earth; therefore, we resolve that we, gathered here today, will become such a group. We earnestly wish and hope that the groups of unification scattered around the world will also be allowed to resolve in such a position.

We thank you for this meeting at such a time, and we hope once again that you will not remain in a sorrowful position. Please cover us, who are full of flaws, with your infinite mercy, compassion, and grace, and cultivate the image of the new precious child that we have imagined for the future, so that we may become the ancestors of faith, holding the torch of faith to illuminate the world of darkness and at the same time become heavenly warriors who can conquer the world of darkness, and let this time be a time when we resolve in our hearts to become the army of justice. Please remember each one of us so that we may remain as your descendants who can fulfill the promise of the future.

Now, the groups of unification will become the embodiments of faith, centered around the sons standing here, removing the foundation of distrust at the family, tribal, national levels, and will surely become the embodiment of your unwavering hope, holding the new sprouts of your eternal faith. When the nations of the world are transformed into the heavenly kingdom through them, we know that a new culture will be established through them, so we earnestly ask and wish that this time will be a time of such resolution.

I ask once again that your will and desire be realized with us and that it may be victorious on the foundation of your faith. I pray all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.

I hope that we will once again resolve in our hearts to become the ancestors of faith. Then we will all stand up and conclude with a triumphant shout. 
Unification Church, Hooray! Hooray! Hooray! Victory for the warriors of unification, Hooray! Hooray! Hooray! Hooray for True Parents! Hooray! Hooray! Hooray! "Hooray for True Parents! Hooray! Hooray! Hooray!"*

What we must do in the future
You must understand how significant the responsibilities of the church leaders in our homeland, or even more so, of those of you who are leading the way, are. Although it may not be apparent now, it is becoming the nourishment and foundation of history.

What Abel needs is to restore the parents.
The history of restoration is a history of indemnity and restoration; therefore, to restore, there must be a process of sacrifice. Sacrifice is necessary. When you take on the responsibilities as church leaders or group leaders before the will, it means you are taking on a central responsibility in the history of restoration.

From a principled perspective, those who take on central responsibilities are in the position of Abel. Today, in our Unification Church, we are called Abel in relation to the established churches, we call the blessed families Abel within our church, and among the blessed families, we refer to the long-established 36 families as Abel. The more established a person is, the more they are considered to be closer to heaven. However, you must understand that the existence of Abel cannot be without Cain.

What Abel needs is to restore the parents. It is to restore the fallen Adam and Eve to their original state. In other words, Abel came into existence to restore the parents. Of course, if Adam and Eve had not fallen, there would be no need for Abel or Cain, but because they fell, we must restore the parents through the existence of Abel. Only when the parents are restored and Abel and Cain become completely one with the parents can they rise to the original standard that is free from the fall.

Since Adam and Eve fell centered on love, even if we have established families and have taken on the form of a son-in-law in our process of restoration today, that position is not the position of completion. No matter how much we have established families, that period is one that must exceed the standard of completion of the growth stage, and you must understand this.

At this point (pointing to the board), we must move toward the period of completion. In other words, we must go through the completion of the growth stage, the completion of the maturity stage, and the completion of the perfection stage. Our human ancestors lost everything due to the fall at the level of the completion of the growth stage; they lost their substance and lost love. Therefore, all these issues must be indemnified and restored in this process.

To say that love was lost here means that false parents emerged. Because love was lost, we must stand in a position where we can establish a relationship with the True Parents, but to establish the position of True Parents, true Cain and Abel must emerge who can be united and restored.

The significance of the Unification Church's blessing
Here (pointing to the board), in order to ascend while becoming one with the parents, we must find everything that was lost due to the fall. By losing the love of the parents, humanity has lost the Day of Parents and the Day of Children. By losing the Day of Parents, we have lost the Day of Children and the Day of All Things. Humanity has lost everything due to the fall. Therefore, we must rise up from here to find what was lost.

The Day of Parents spoken of in the Unification Church is established when we settle the relationship of True Parents after resolving the issues of having become false parents centered on love. After finding the Day of Parents, we must find the Day of Children. We must not only find the Day of Parents. We must surpass all conditions of indemnity and restoration as children. Thus, the Day of Children is established. Furthermore, by the parents and children becoming one, the Day of All Things is established in the meaning that all things have been restored. We must establish these three significant days of restoration and ascend to this point (the level of completion of perfection). (Pointing to the board)

The Day of God is the position where one can meet God; it is not the position of the completion stage of the growth level but the position of the completion stage of perfection. When one stands at the original level of completion of perfection, one is bound to become one with God. However, because of the fall, humanity fell at the level of the completion of the growth stage, and therefore we must restore the completion of the growth stage.

Standing in such a position is the blessing of our Unification Church. To say that one has received a blessing prayer means that one has received it at this level (the level of completion of the growth stage). Because Adam and Eve fell from this position, humanity must rise again from this fallen position.

However, to rise to this position, one cannot go alone. Because Adam and Eve fell together, today on the path of restoration, they must rise together. A couple who has completely united centered on God must emerge to surpass the level of completion of the growth stage. While there are various specific contents of indemnity regarding the children of faith, I will omit them due to time constraints.

First, we must surpass this position (the level of completion of the growth stage). You all know that the blessing of the Unification Church is for the purpose of surpassing this position.

So, after being blessed, does everything end? It does not end. Through the blessing, as citizens of the heavenly kingdom, we establish a truly horizontal relationship where humanity and God can cooperate for the first time. It is through the blessing that such a relationship is established. Therefore, you must understand that before this, humanity could not stand in a position to relate to God.

The reason we must establish children of faith
Originally, if Adam and Eve had not fallen, there would have to be three archangels centered on Adam and Eve. Thus, Adam and Eve must completely unite with the three archangels centered on God, looking up to the level of completion of perfection. However, because the angels fell, they became Satan and caused humanity to fall backwards. In order to restore this, we must go through the three stages and three eras of indemnity.

In the creation of Adam and Eve, the three archangels must completely unite and cooperate. In other words, the purpose of the three archangels is to assist in the creation of Adam and Eve. However, Adam and Eve fell. Because Adam and Eve fell, it is God's providence to restore them to the position of Adam and Eve before the fall. Therefore, in order to rise to this position, one must first go through the process of receiving cooperation from the angels. Who must go through this process? It is Cain, Abel, and Seth of the Adam family. These three sons are in the position to indemnify like the three archangels.

Thus, we must ascend from the era of the servant of servants, through the era of the servant, to the era of the adopted son, and finally to the era of the direct lineage. Can we establish a connection with the direct lineage era after completely passing through the era of the servant of servants, the era of the servant, and the era of the adopted son? We cannot simply establish a connection with the direct lineage era. It must be established according to the principle; we must go through the expectation of faith, the expectation of substance, and the expectation for the Messiah. In other words, we must welcome the Messiah. The Messiah is God's True Son. The adopted son and the True Son have different bloodline relationships. Therefore, bloodline transformation is necessary.

That is why the Bible speaks of the grafting process for restoration. In other words, if the wild olive tree is left as it is, it will bear the fruit of the wild olive tree, but if it is grafted onto the true olive tree, it can bear the fruit of the true olive tree. This means that it will give birth to good sons and daughters without original sin.

If we do not completely receive God's love on this earth after giving birth to good sons and daughters without original sin, we cannot enter the kingdom of heaven. This is God's principle of creation, and it is essential to bridge the gap of restoration through the principles.

Then, what does it mean that the form of the three archangels must reappear in a horizontal standard? It means that there must be three sons to restore the parents. Therefore, centered on Adam, Cain, Abel, and even Satan must come together to form the historical connection of the three. You must understand that Adam did not ascend with his three sons but rather fell down. Therefore, in our faith process today, we must understand that we cannot restore unless we find and indemnify all the mistakes made in the past. 

The purpose of establishing children of faith in our Unification Church is to indemnify this process. What are children of faith? Why are children of faith necessary?
If there are no children of faith, there is no way for someone in the position of a faithful parent to rise to the position of a parent before us humans. This is Abel's position. Moreover, Adam and Eve lost their substance due to the Fall. Then they lost their heart. Abel must take on the intermediate responsibility to restore these.

In other words, Adam and Eve, due to the Fall, are in an intermediate position between heaven and Satan. Therefore, they are in a position where they cannot move to either side. Who can keep them on the side of heaven? It is not something Adam and Eve can do. Abel must do it. Therefore, Abel must indemnify all the conditions of accusation that remain in restoring the substance and heart of the parents. You must understand that there must be a connection of indemnity here.

The position of Abel is that the historical offering of blood is not found in Cain, Adam, or the parents. It is found in Abel. Abel's position is that of the archangel. What kind of archangel? An unfallen archangel. You must understand that the archangel, who became Satan and caused the Fall of the entire universe, must bring about indemnity through Abel to restore this.

The history of Israel starting from Jacob
Because Satan is the archangel, Adam is higher than the archangel. Right? If the archangel is a servant, Adam and Eve are direct sons and daughters, so they are higher. Also, God is supposed to directly govern Adam, not the archangel. From this perspective, we must restore the fallen world of individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world.

How is the fallen world? This fallen world is not a world that God can govern. It is a world governed by Satan, the archangel. Therefore, we must separate the connection that allows God to govern the world.

Where is the reason for this separation? It is because God created Adam through the archangel. Therefore, the position that must be separated is the position of the archangel.

In creating Adam, the archangel was the object of God's inquiry, the subject of consultation, and the cooperating object. This is the position of the archangel. If he does not cooperate in making Adam, he becomes aligned with Satan. If he stands in a position of cooperation according to that principle, it is what God takes; if he stands in a position of non-cooperation, he deviates from the principle, and it is managed by the non-principled Satan.

Therefore, if one stands in a principled position within the world of Satan, God can take him away. In other words, as long as one can establish the conditions and environment that can present the elements for Adam to be re-created, God will take him away. To do this, the history of Judaism has been carried out over 4,000 years since the Fall of humanity.

The history of servants is that the age of servants is the age when God can be called the master, but the age of the servant of servants is the age when the servant is called the master. It is always like that. If one cannot establish a foundation of expectation at any time, God cannot establish His foothold. Do you understand? No matter how much an individual establishes a foothold, if that individual dies, it is over. One must establish a foothold on this earth by fulfilling the foundation of expectation. You cannot rise up if you cannot do it. It is something you will never be able to do.

And the heavenly lineage must be better than the historical lineage of the Satanic world to ascend. Isn't that how it should be? Satan sets conditions when it comes to being in a position lower than himself. When Satan is in a position lower than himself, he claims ownership. That is the principle.

Because we were born into this world, in order to escape from this world, a person surrounded within the boundaries must become a stronger entity than the power of the fence; otherwise, there is no way to escape. In other words, when one becomes weaker than the counterpart, one is always subject to that counterpart. However, when one becomes stronger than the counterpart, one can escape from there. That is the conclusion.

Principle of Existence, Action, and Development
To develop, one must always seek a position that is better than oneself. In other words, action occurs only in places where one can become a plus, not in places that become a minus. Isn’t that right? There can only be development when two become one; if they do not become one, there will absolutely be no development. You must clearly understand that this is the ironclad rule of the universe. To become one, each must discover values that can be plus. If they become one in a situation that leads to a minus, if that is a principle, then this world would cease to exist. Do you understand what I mean? If there is a principle of becoming one in a diminishing manner, then this world would turn upside down. If the principle of the world is such, then even if one side is formed, the other side will collapse. Do you understand? Such principles do not exist.

All things must develop, and development cannot occur without the relationship between subject and object. Action does not arise. In today's world of existence, when we ask whether existence comes first or power comes first, the necessity of existence is a well-known fact. However, to exist, power must be present. In other words, when we ask whether existence comes first or power comes first, no matter how absurd it may sound, we do not say that existence comes first. Power must exist for existence to be present.

What exists can be seen. However, power is invisible. Power symbolizes mental strength. Therefore, materialists cannot claim that matter is fundamental. Existence itself is power, but power is not visible. The invisible is what constitutes power.

Is existence merely blind existence? To exist, power must be present. Is power just sitting there? No. For power to exist, it must continually act. Only then does power emerge. In other words, for power to exist, action must be present.

Then, to sustain power through continuous action, how must action be carried out? It cannot act alone. There must be both subject and object. This is the ironclad rule. In the action between subject and object, it does not simply act as it is; it acts only when a place that can be better than the positions of subject and object is discovered. This is the principle.

There are five pluses and five minuses, and if there is something that can combine to make eleven or twelve, then action occurs. When such action takes place, something new is created. If there is something greater, action occurs, but if there is only one, it may stop at the corresponding action of one or remain in a certain situation, leading to a disintegration action. This is the principle of the universe. Therefore, in the exchange between subject and object, action occurs only when something better can be discovered; otherwise, action does not take place. You must understand that this is the ironclad rule of the universe.

In a chemical experiment, there are some elements that cannot combine even if various chemicals are added and all sorts of tricks are performed. Even if they are said to combine, they become a minus. When they act, they both become a minus, so they absolutely do not act. God also does not allow action to occur. Action does not unfold. That is the principle.

However, there are some elements that, unexpectedly, do act together. When they interact, they must form something greater, something that can be more plus, which is why they act. No matter how much you try to prevent it, they will act. This is the principle. This is the principle of cosmic formation. Today, we are not aware of this.

What the Messiah Must Do

The coming of the Messiah is to save the world. Originally, if during the time of Jesus, the Israelite people and Judaism had united with Jesus and formed a sovereign nation that could proudly stand against the Roman Empire, God would have directly governed it.

However, because there has been no nation on the side of heaven that can establish the dignity and face of heaven until now, we must understand that countless Christians have gone through a tragic historical process of being slaughtered and sacrificed without being able to intervene. Therefore, the nation is the problem. You must also understand that you are in such a position. That is why what all Christians around the world should earnestly desire is to find a nation.
하여 야곱이 장자의 기업을 받을 수 있는 길을 열어주게 됩니다. 이렇게 해서 야곱은 장자의 기업을 복귀하게 되는 것입니다.

이러한 복귀의 과정에서 야곱은 아벨의 입장을 복귀해야 하는 책임을 지고 있습니다. 그는 아벨의 실수를 대신 탕감해야 하며, 동시에 아담이 천사장에게 굴복한 것을 복귀해야 합니다. 야곱은 두 사람 모두의 사명을 가지고 있는 것입니다. 다시 말해, 그는 아담이 천사에게 굴복당한 것을 복귀할 책임이 있으며, 가인이 아벨을 죽인 것을 복귀할 사명이 있습니다.

이런 원리적인 입장에서 보면, 원리를 어긴 사탄 편의 것을 복귀하기 위해서는 그 반대의 경로를 통해야 합니다. 해와와 가인이 하나의 자리에 섰기 때문에 사망이 결정된 것입니다. 그러므로 리브가는 해와와 같은 입장에서, 아버지 이삭을 속이고 아들 에서를 속여야 합니다. 리브가는 해와 대신으로서 이삭과 에서를 속였습니다.

하나님은 이러한 속임수를 통해 복귀의 섭리를 이루어 가고 있습니다. 이것은 불가피한 현상으로, 반대의 경로를 통해 복귀할 수 있는 길이 없기 때문입니다. 그러므로 리브가가 야곱을 세워 축복을 받게 하는 것은 지극히 당연한 일입니다.

어머니와 아들이 하나됨으로써 망했던 죄악의 결과는, 하늘 편적 어머니와 하늘 편적 아들이 하나됨으로써 청산할 수 있는 복귀의 길이 열리는 것입니다. 리브가가 에서와 야곱을 배었을 때, 복중에서 둘이 싸우게 됩니다. 작은아들 자리에 있는 동생이 큰아들 자리에 먼저 서야 하는데, 엉뚱한 사탄의 자식이 장자의 자리에 서 있으니 싸우게 마련입니다. 

리브가는 하나님께 기도하며 “내 복중에서 싸우는 것을 어찌하리이까?” 하고 묻습니다. 하나님은 “네 복중에는 두 나라가 있으며, 큰 자가 작은 자를 섬기리라.”고 말씀하셨습니다. 이것이 공식입니다. 이 원칙에서 모든 것이 풀려나가는 것입니다.

야곱은 장자 기업을 복귀하기 위해 하나님 편에 돌아가고자 했습니다. 그는 아담 대신 책임을 져야 하기에 누구보다도 장자의 기업을 사모한 자입니다. 반면 에서는 현실주의자로, 하나님의 뜻을 모르고 배를 위해 사는 사람이었습니다. 그러나 야곱은 장자의 기업, 즉 하나님의 축복을 받은 사람이 복 받는 것임을 알았습니다. 그래서 그는 에서에게 장자의 기업을 사는 거래를 하게 됩니다. 

이렇게 샀기 때문에 장자의 기업은 산 사람이 갖게 되는 것입니다. 리브가와 야곱은 원리원칙을 가려서 야곱이 장자의 기업을 받을 수 있는 길을 열어주게 됩니다.
