If they stay in America for a year and a half or two years, they will master English. Once they master English, they can go to France, and in just a year, they will be fluent in French. 
Then, after that, they can learn Spanish in just a year…. Since we have an organization, if the teacher just signs, everything will be possible. “Hey, French leader, feed this person.” When that happens, they will say, “Thank you for sending such a command postcard.” Then they will ask, “Should we choose a first-class hotel or a second-class hotel? Where should we choose?” Such times will come in the not-so-distant future. 
After that, to learn Spanish, they just need to stay in Spain for one year. If they come out with just one language from each country, they will be able to evangelize anywhere. Do you understand? So, don’t you want to become a champion of the task force? 
At that time, if an outstanding wife is in the task force, the husbands will have no choice but to follow. (Laughter) If the husbands are outstanding, the wives will have no choice but to follow the husbands in the task force. They can live in the country where their husband wants to live, or the wife can live in the country where she wants to live. If they want to live in America, they can go live in America; if they want to live in Germany, they can go live in Germany…. Wherever they go, in places where there are Unification Church members, they will be welcomed with open arms, saying, “Welcome! You are a precious person coming to revive our country; please come.” Will that happen or not? 
From now on, I will extract outstanding members of the task force and take them on a world tour, and wherever they go, I will say, “Hey, guide them.” I will provide a bus for them. I will send a group of about 40 people with global achievements to America and make them compete, saying, “Hey, take America!” This is how we will evangelize by showing them examples and coaching them. This is the plan of the teacher to establish a unified global activity. Do you understand? “Yes.” You don’t have to worry about money. I will earn the money. There is plenty of money. 
Just hearing this makes me feel like I don’t even know if I’m hungry without lunch. Right? “Yes.” This is not a public discussion. So, to make this happen globally in the future, we need to establish the headquarters in America. Right? We need to set up the headquarters in America, and I will become the commander-in-chief and push down from the top so that you all can receive plenty of supplies in the future…. Right? (Laughter) Isn’t that right, our lovely ones? Even if you dislike me, you should look kindly upon me because you have suffered for my sake. Right? Parents naturally love their children who have struggled more than the children of noble families who ride horses. From that perspective, since we have all struggled together…. 
But now the church is worried. Even if they have to suffer like this, they say, “Teacher, I have suffered this much and followed this much, but I feel upset because I have nothing.” Do they say that? 
Everyone, on May 9, 1972, the teacher told me to leave my house, and while I was following him, I said, “What has happened that I have no results?” Have I ever said that? Did I put conditions saying I suffered for you? You little brats, I stand above you. 
“Even though I have nothing now, you told me to follow you, and now you don’t recognize me? Aang Aang!” (Laughter) Do you want to do that or not? “I won’t do that.” Since I went out because of you, can I say I won’t do that? In that position, it’s still okay. (Laughter) If you just think of the teacher, that’s how it is. 
However, the teacher is doing more advanced work than you, so there will be no benefit from that. (Laughter) If the teacher does it for himself, you would resent him, but from the standpoint of doing it for a bigger issue than you, there is no benefit. That is the traditional path that Abel must take. Do you understand? “Yes.” The teacher has played that game too. 
I am not thinking about becoming successful now. Although I am living like this, I have done all that I need to do. I have done all my duties. When I start talking, I can go on for seven hours, ten hours, or even twelve hours if I take a meal break, and then I run out of words. When I run out of words, I speak like the sound of air circulating in a tank. But I have fulfilled my duties. 
I have done all my duties in Japan as well. That’s why even though I planned to come back after 15 days, I left within 15 days without feeling any guilt of conscience. If I have time, even if someone comes in late at night when they should be sleeping, I talk to them as if I am representing all the Japanese members; I never chased anyone away saying I was tired. Even if it was late at night, I told them to stay a little longer before leaving. That’s how I came back. That’s why I don’t have any guilt of conscience. When I die, if I stand before the Father from the standpoint of having done all I could, the Father will not be unaware of that. That’s how I am thinking now. I have been busy living from morning until now since I came here. So, you all must not say, “I won’t go.” 
Solutions to the Economic Problems of the American Church 
One good news I want to share with you is about the plan I made this time. In the future, we will establish a tradition of actively supporting Americans through Asians. This is the teacher’s future strategy. To do this, who should we use among Asians? Koreans are struggling with economic issues. Moreover, due to national conditions, going abroad requires visas and passports. Because dollars are consumed, they are trying not to send people out as much as possible. So, how difficult is that? 
However, in Japan, if an invitation comes, a passport can be issued within three days, and the passport is valid for four years. Therefore, they can go out anytime. And they can take unlimited amounts of money with them. Because of this position, we are promoting Japan as a representative of Asians. Additionally, since Japan is a land of the rising sun, it has the responsibility to serve the world as a mother, so it must provide for everyone by sacrificing its blood and flesh. Everything must go through the mother’s touch to develop. Therefore, the teacher’s plan is to establish a tradition by promoting Japan as a representative of Asians. Do you understand? 
In America, what is happening is that there is something called cleaning service. In American households, both men and women work. Since everyone goes to work, many homes are left empty during the day. Therefore, cleaning becomes an issue. Currently, mostly Black women are doing this cleaning, but the cleaning service is a specialized cleaning technique. Our members have researched attractive cleaning methods that can be done simply, even with pillars. When I went to see it, it was incredibly clean…. 
They call it a cleaning service, and if you work just four hours a day, you can earn an average of $40. Do you understand? If you work just four hours a day, you can earn $40. The food expenses are not much. They estimate food expenses to be between $35 and $50. Since they live together, it doesn’t cost much. When you look at it this way, surely one person can earn at least $30 by working just four hours. 
So, how many people do we need to mobilize? In Washington alone, we need not just thousands but tens of thousands. Do you understand? If we expand to New York or nationwide, we will need millions. So, we need to lay the foundation quickly. 
We will not only do cleaning but also painting, buying houses, repairing them, and selling them. So, we are currently organizing a real estate company. We will expand this nationwide and buy houses to put them under double mortgages. The selling company will mortgage the house to the bank to pull out money, and the buying company will also mortgage the house to pull out money, effectively doubling the funds. By doing this, the value of the house will exceed twice its original price. Do you understand? This is the business we want to do. 
If we can do this, we estimate that if we invest just $300,000, we will receive over $20 million within five years. We have now instructed a plan to secure funding in America within three years or five years. 
So, to do the cleaning service, since New York is the largest, we have instructed to buy a house in New York to lay the foundation. We are currently working on that. We aim to create a place where at least hundreds of people can move in and receive training, and a very nice center for our association will emerge in New York. That place is a house where the richest person in New York used to live; it’s an incredible location. We are currently planning to buy it. 
So, we will train everyone there. First, we will select twelve representative people from among the Japanese members who are skilled in business and educate them, integrating them into twelve cities. Then, by the end of this year, we will send 120 people, ten from each of the twelve. The twelve people will train ten each. This movement will then branch out, and as it branches out, it will form a national organization. 
After this, if we mobilize more than 400 or about 600 people, I believe this will spread nationwide. Since America has 50 states, if we send just ten people from each state, that will be 500 people. First, we just need to gather more than 400 people. Isn’t that possible? 400 to 600 people, within that limit, we will send ten people from each state to establish that tradition. After that, what will we do? We will have to collaborate with Europeans and operate in America. 
Some Europeans may not speak English. Regardless of their university education, they will need to study English for two years. Only then can they attend lectures at universities. During those two years of studying English, if they do it at home, there are no limits. Therefore, in our cleaning service, if we have someone who speaks English as a guide, it doesn’t matter if they can’t speak much. They will go and do the cleaning. Good morning or good afternoon…
You just need to say "afternoon" and "goodbye." (Laughter) When the other person asks you to speak, you can say, "Oh, I have to work on this." (Laughter) Because of this, if you know a few words, you can conduct a business that is a hundred percent more efficient than the person speaking. This is what God has blessed… well, I will manage with locusts, quails, and manna in the wilderness while eating them leisurely. (Laughter) So, if we can mobilize 300 to 400 people, if each person earns just $30, that amounts to $12,000 a day. Therefore, in a year, it exceeds $4 million. With $4 million, we can provide all the funds needed for all the active members in the United States and still have some left over.

By doing this, we will push out all the ones who can speak English in the U.S. The Japanese will all earn money, while the Americans will go out and fight. So, when we engage in the movement to dismantle established churches, many will join us. In the fall, when the rice is well-ripened, like a bat, if you hit it against a white stone, it will fall off in a shower, right? That’s how it will be. Right now, the hippies are causing a stir in the established churches. In this chaotic situation, we are the unified hippies. We are just like the hippies. They ask where the kingdom of God is, where the family is, and where the mother and father are. But the unified hippies are entirely different from them, as they appear anew for the sake of the nation, for the family, and for the ideal brothers.

On one hand, they are struggling, looking disheveled, while we are marching with trumpets, which fits the temperament of the Americans.

Japanese family earns money while American family evangelizes.
During our tour in the U.S., our bus broke down, and the engine blew up. The repair cost $3,500. On top of that, we were running out of food expenses on the road, so we had no choice. But they are masterpieces. Since my mother took us around for revival meetings, we organized the chorus well. So, at such times, we expanded our evangelism in every possible way and instilled the need for self-reliance. During that time, we were taught to do all sorts of things. We begged, did everything, and engaged in all kinds of antics.

However, that day, a famous chorus was supposed to come to that city. So, all the citizens gathered in the auditorium, but the chorus had an accident and couldn’t come. Wow! This is God’s protection, so it makes sense! (Laughter) "Then our group will do it. Our chorus can do anything. We can perform for not just two hours but ten hours." That’s what we said. How well have our group been trained? With that, we got energized, and it became a big deal with radio broadcasts and everything. We made contact with all the citizens of that city. It was reported in the newspapers, so it became widely known at once.

As a result, the mayor, some mothers, and all sorts of people came out, and they cooperated, saying that this is a significant event in our street and that we should work together. They repaired everything, and we ended up with some money left over.

What kind of country is America? If a profit of $50 million is made, and it is donated entirely to a public service organization, there is not a single cent of tax. This is the system in place. In some cases, the tax can be one and a half times the profit. Do you understand? At that time, they secretly go around saying, "Hey, let’s donate." Then, all the taxes are waived, so the company survives, the owner is happy, and we benefit from the donations… There are countless such occurrences.

Because of this, groups have emerged that negotiate from behind the scenes. At such times, when the trumpet sounds globally, and the One World Crusade or whatever is in the air, money will come not in bundles but by truckloads. (Laughter) You might think that’s okay.

So, by mobilizing the Japanese people to establish a tradition of economic support, Americans will spread churches worldwide… In America, wherever you go, when you talk about the Bible, both adults and children all nod in agreement. There is no one who doesn’t know the Bible. When I came to Japan, I found that people are in the dark about the Bible, but they have already been well-educated within the Christian cultural sphere, so if we just focus on the idea of the Second Coming and instill a worldview, they can all ride like a galloping steed. They are well-prepared.

In America, two-thirds of the population is on the Christian list. 120 million people are practically all Christians. If we set fire to this and it catches, it will be the teacher who ends up with a pile of money, and we will have to flee. Moreover, America is all about dove-ism. Grandparents raise their children and send them off to marry, and since they can’t maintain a big house, they sell it and buy apartments, so many people live off the money they’ve saved. Given this situation, there will be plenty of money in the future.

Therefore, the global mobilization of your generation will be quite good. To lead this, I will gather world-renowned figures in science, economics, politics, culture, media, and religion, and I plan to organize a global brain organization centered around these five fields, like the True Parents. So, I am trying to push forward with the "World Peace Unification Federation," which I planned three years ago. It will start this October. Do you understand? I am currently working on this vast plan.

You should not think like a frog in a well. We must become a revolutionary force that can influence the nation and can restore the nation and sovereignty. Only then can we be proud on the world stage; we must not be like communists, always struggling and weak. Do you understand? "Yes." With this mindset, all of you… This is not for individual promotion.

Economic recovery plan for Japan.
Next, let me talk about Japan. Since Japan has a population of 100 million, if we assume five people per household, that makes 20 million households. My plan is to seize the economy of these 20 million households in the not-so-distant future. This is possible.

Let’s look at Mitsubishi and Mitsui. What plans do they have? They aim to mobilize about 3,000 people within three years, which will be around 1976… So, by the end of the three 7-year courses, mobilizing 70,000 people in the business sector is feasible. If we do this, with my special mission, if each person manages 300 households, that’s 21 million households. So, each person will be a dispatched member visiting 300 households every day. What will they do from morning till evening? They will take orders to deliver all consumables.

If we can secure 300 households nationwide based on this national foundation, we will know everything, even if an ant gets into a fight and breaks its leg in any household. Do you understand what I mean? Counting chopsticks is insufficient. If we know that an ant broke its leg in a fight, we can know even more.

Once we set this up, how will we deliver everything? We will take orders through our company from the production site and deliver directly nationwide. For this, a large building needs to be established. Through a nationwide communication network, we will organize everything, saying, "We have so many households in such and such a military." We need to designate 70,000 people to engage in nationwide activities.

If we can deliver just 300 households, we will buy goods at cost from the production site. The profit will only be slightly more than the cost. By leaving as small a profit as possible and starting to share everything, we will completely lay the foundation within a year. If we proceed like this, all departments will collapse due to our operation. All the big stores will have to close down. In this case, there will be demonstrations against the Unification Church. Even the communists will demonstrate. But let’s see, you guys! The time has already passed. So, you can sell cheap if you want…

"We are doing this for the benefit of the people. This is a public service for the benefit of the nation rather than for individual profit." We will confidently promote this on the radio. "Because our theory is like this, we are serving so that the public can benefit, so take two-thirds of the remaining price." If that happens, the departments will collapse. They will all disappear.

If this happens, if we can control at least half or one-third of the national consumption of any major company's specialty products, if the price is high at the production site, we will say, "Hey, lower this price a bit." We will only add a little profit to the cost. We will leave just enough profit for the factory workers to eat. By doing this, I will take over the Japanese economy within a few years, train them all, and redirect them all to America. Then, I will expand the territory in America and create a global organization to seize the world economy.

By laying this foundation, while I am still here, if I say to the members in America, "Don’t buy Ford cars, buy Japanese Toyota cars!" the Ford cars will not sell. Right? Even if the national sovereignty is restricted, we will not be stopped. Just show that we can create finances that can be sold in that country despite the high taxes. The world economy will be in my hands. This is what I intend to do.

To do this, I am currently… If I train just 7,000 people in Japan, and if those 7,000 train ten people each, we will immediately secure 70,000 people. Then, if we organize a nationwide structure and proceed smoothly, all the money will come in according to our plan. America should not make a fuss.

The poor people suffering in the Unification Church, I will make you prosperous. Are you feeling good or bad? Will I make you prosperous, or do you want to be prosperous? Why aren’t you answering? You will be, right? Will I make it happen? "Please make it happen." This is the traditional habit of a small nation. They all lack a spirit of self-reliance.

If you earned money, did you earn it for Korea? You earned it for the world. Don’t even think about it. So, stand in a position where you fought for the world before that time comes. If you stand in a position where you can fight for the world, you will receive help. Do you understand? If you prepare your own funds and do this and that, there will be nothing left. Do you understand? "Yes."

So, I am planning a four-year training program for these 7,000 agents in Japan. If it takes two more years, after six years, everything I plan will come to fruition. Therefore, I intend to produce and sell a lot of ginseng tea.

Now, because of us, problems have arisen in the Japanese Ministry of International Trade and Industry. Problems have also arisen in the police department. The merchants say that the salespeople from the Unification Church are terrifying. It is astonishing that women who have received no training can sell so well. While department stores can only achieve sales of about 20,000 yen a day, we can achieve 15, 20, or even 30 times that. So, we are recording sales of up to 600,000 yen. The ideology is frightening. Do you understand? "Yes."

To carry out such activities, I urge you all to study English in the future. So, prepare to go abroad. And when you go, you should be able to cross borders without any restrictions. Oh, I feel bored when I travel. Who made visas and all that… It feels very unpleasant. Understand this, and be prepared to sacrifice for such a country, for the day of national liberation, and I hope you will become dignified pioneers of today with the hope of tomorrow. Shall I take a little break? "Yes."

<Prayer> We have clearly understood what the decisive foundation of your protection and your infinite providence is on this earth. We must realize how miserable it is to be a people without a nation and how absurd it is to have a destiny without a nation. We must understand how astonishing it is that we have come to recognize this fact once again.

Therefore, we must lay this foundation, and our activities to expand this foundation must be truly meticulous and multidimensional. When we realize that this is our mission, we will become your sons and daughters who will run ahead, undeterred by any difficulties, and fight fiercely to lay that foundation. I earnestly ask you to allow this vow to be a vow of responsibility in this era faced with the solemn fate of the nation.

Please guide us in the path of this poor nation and us, and accompany us with your guidance as we walk this path. I earnestly ask you to unite us in a position where the destiny of this nation can align with the providential destiny you have granted. I offer all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen. *
